\pm \int_{r_0}^r \frac{r}{r - 2} dr, \\ t &amp;= \pm \int_{r_0}^r \frac{r}{r - 2} dr \\ &amp;= \pm \int_{r_0}^r \frac{r - 2 + 2}{r - 2} dr \\ &amp;= \pm \int_{r_0}^r \left(1 + \frac{2}{r - 2}\right) scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow></mrow></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><mrow></mrow><mo>=</mo><mo>±</mo><msubsup><mrow><mo fence="true">[</mo><mi>r</mi><mo>+</mo><mn>2</mn><mi>ln</mi><mo>⁡</mo><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mn>2</mn><mo>−</mo><mi>r</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo \begin{align*} t &amp;= \pm \int_{r_0}^r \frac{r}{r - 2} dr \\ &amp;= \pm \int_{r_0}^r \frac{- r}{2 - r} dr \\ &amp;= \pm \int_{r_0}^r \frac{2 - r - 2}{2 - r} dr \\ &amp;= \pm \int_{r_0}^r \left(1 - \frac{2}{2 - r}\right) dr \\ &amp;= \pm \int_{r_0}^r -\left(- 1 + \frac{2}{2 - r}\right) dr, \\ u &amp;= 2 - r, \\ du &amp;= -dr, \\ t &amp;= \pm \int_{2 - r_0}^{2 - r} \left(- 1 + \frac{2}{u}\right) du \\ &amp;= \pm \left[-u + 2 \ln u\right]_{2 - r_0}^{2 - r} \\ &amp;= \pm \left[-2 + r + 2 \ln (2 -r)\right]_{r_0}^r \qquad \textrm{constants cancel in definite integrals} \\ &amp;= \pm \left[r + 2 \ln (2 -r)\right]_{r_0}^r. \\ \end{align*} </annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" fence="true">(</mo><msup><mi>U</mi><mn>0</mn></msup><mfrac><mrow><mi>r</mi><mo>−</mo><mn>2</mn></mrow><mi>r</mi></mfrac><mo fence="true">)</mo></mrow></mrow></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><msup><mi>U</mi><mn>0</mn></msup><mfrac><mrow><mi>r</mi><mo>−</mo><mn>2</mn></mrow><mi>r</mi></mfrac></mrow></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><mrow></mrow><mo>=</mo><msup><mi>e</mi><mi>C</mi></msup><mo separator="true">,</mo></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr></mtable><annotation encoding="application/x-tex"> \begin{align*} \frac{d^2 t}{d\lambda^2} + \frac{2}{r(r - 2)} \frac{dt}{d\lambda} \frac{dr}{d\lambda} &amp;= 0, \qquad \frac{dt}{d\lambda} = U^0, \\ \frac{dU^0}{d\lambda} + \frac{2}{r(r - 2)} \frac{dr}{d\lambda} U^0 &amp;= 0, \\ \frac{1}{U^0} dU^0 + \frac{2}{r(r - 2)} dr &amp;= 0, \\ \int \frac{1}{U^0} dU^0 + \int \frac{2}{r(r - 2)} dr &amp;= C, \\ \ln U^0 + \int \left(\frac{1}{r - 2} - \frac{1}{r}\right) dr &amp;= C, \\ \ln U^0 + \ln (r - 2) - \ln(r) &amp;= C, \\ \ln \left(U^0 \frac{r - 2}{r}\right) &amp;= C, \\ U^0 \frac{r - 2}{r} &amp;= e^C, \end{align*} \begin{align*} \frac{d^2 \phi}{d\lambda^2} + \frac{2}{r} \frac{dr}{d\lambda} \frac{d\phi}{d\lambda} &amp;= 0, \qquad \frac{d\phi}{d\lambda} = U^3, \\ \frac{dU^3}{d\lambda} + \frac{2}{r} \frac{dr}{d\lambda} U^3 &amp;= 0, \\ \frac{1}{U^3} dU^3 + \frac{2}{r} dr &amp;= 0, \\ \int \frac{1}{U^3} dU^3 + \int \frac{2}{r} dr &amp;= C, \\ \ln U^3 + 2\ln r &amp;= C, \\ \ln (U^3 r^2) &amp;= C, \\ U^3 r^2 &amp;= e^C, \\ \end{align*} </annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" \frac{r}{r - 2} \left(\frac{dr}{d\lambda}\right)^2 + \frac{\mathcal{L}^2}{r^2}, \\ 0 &amp;= -\frac{r}{r - 2} \mathcal{E}^2 + \frac{r}{r - 2} \left(\frac{dr}{d\lambda}\right)^2 + \frac{\mathcal{L}^2}{r^2} - \epsilon, \\ 0 &amp;= - \mathcal{E}^2 + \left(\frac{dr}{d\lambda}\right)^2 + \frac{r - 2}{r} \frac{\mathcal{L}^2}{r^2} - \frac{r - 2}{r} \epsilon, \\ 0 &amp;= - \mathcal{E}^2 + \left(\frac{dr}{d\lambda}\right)^2 + \left(1 - \frac{2}{r}\right) \left(\frac{\mathcal{L}^2}{r^2} - \epsilon\right), \\ \mathcal{E}^2 &amp;= \left(\frac{dr}{d\lambda}\right)^2 + \left(1 - \frac{2}{r}\right) \left(\frac{\mathcal{L}^2}{r^2} - \epsilon\right), \\ &amp;= \left(\frac{dr}{d\lambda}\right)^2 + \left(\frac{\mathcal{L}^2}{r^2} - \frac{2\mathcal{L}^2}{r^3} + \frac{2}{r} \epsilon - \epsilon\right), \\ &amp;= \left(\frac{dr}{d\lambda}\right)^2 + \frac{\mathcal{L}^2}{r^2} - \frac{2\mathcal{L}^2}{r^3} + \frac{2}{r} \epsilon - \epsilon, \end{align*} \mathcal{L}^2\right)^2 - 4 (m) (3 m \mathcal{L}^2) \\ &amp;= m^2 \mathcal{L}^4 - 12 m^2 \mathcal{L}^2, \\ r &amp;= \frac{-(-m \mathcal{L}^2) \pm \sqrt{m^2 \mathcal{L}^4 - 12 m^2 \mathcal{L}^2}}{2m} \\
